name:V‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçk
info:Business Twin Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:3.2
posted:Posted February 4, 2024
msg:Hotel room: 0 (zero) star
Hotel location: 4 (four) stars
Hotel staff services: 5 (five stars)

We checked into a room on 1/25/2024 for a 6-night stay.  We realized the room smelled smoke even though we requested a non-smoking room.  The worst was the bathroom's strong, moldy, foul smell, which is a health hazard and unacceptable.  On top of it, the in-room HVAC thermostat doesn't work, which we didn't notice until the next morning.  We suffered without fresh air circulation and high room temperature all night long.

The following day, thanks to the friendly, accommodating front desk staff, we could change to another room with no issues like the previous one.  Even the room we changed to also has maintenance issues, such as the ceiling light above the nightstand hanging loose from the ceiling and exploding electrical wires.  And the bathroom Faucet is loose, etc., unfortunately.

Besides the exceptional overall staff services, the hotel is conveniently located in a local neighborhood, a perfect alternative for tourists who want to experience the truth of Guangzhou.  Suppose Baiyun Hotel is positioned as an international five-star hotel.  In that case, besides sustaining excellent staff services, improving room maintenance, upgrading the aging hotel, and paying attention to the details is essential.  Outstanding staff service or a profound hotel history couldn't substitute necessities such as an operational thermostat or a foul smell in the bathroom.

Having said that, I wouldn't consider Baiyun Hotel when we visit Guangzhou next time, nor would I recommend it to others due to my experiences with the hotel room.
----------------------------------------

It was unaffordable to live there at that time, but checking in 50 years later seems like a familiar place. Although it was newly renovated in 2019, you can still feel the strong historical a**osphere. This is also because she is located in the central city that has not been changed for more than 2,000 years. It takes more than 30 minutes to get here from the airport and costs just over 100 yuan. There is a subway station more than 100 meters away from the hotel door, and there are more than 20 ground buses, so transportation is very convenient. In an old five-star hotel, the service is still so rigorous. Although it is not as luxurious as the newly built hotels of the same specification, it has all the facilities and is extremely cost-effective. The catering focuses on Cantonese cuisine, as well as Indian cuisine and seafood buffet (the fried foie gras is great).
In addition, the hotel corridors and bridges are connected to La Park Shopping Center and Youyi Store, making shopping extremely convenient.

Whether it is a celadon vase or framed paintings and calligraphy, they are all unexpected surprises, adding an elegant and gentle a**osphere.
Breakfast is in the buffet restaurant on the top floor. It has a rich variety and the taste can only be said to be useless, but it is convenient and trouble-free. The glass curtain wall overlooks the railing, and the scenery is excellent. You can have a panoramic view of the older generation city center of Guangzhou.
Due to changes in my itinerary, I only stayed for one day, but if I come to Guangzhou next time, Baiyun Hotel will still be my first choice.

msg:Baiyun Hotel is regarded as a traditional hotel in Guangzhou. This time I was just looking for a place to work overtime and take a walk with the baby. It was the first time I stayed here. After staying here, I think it is worth recommending.
First of all, the sleeping environment is comfortable. I am very sensitive to the sleeping environment, even if I feel a little uncomfortable, I will not sleep well. The word "comfortable" is used because the sleeping environment in the room at night, including mattresses, quilts, and pillows, is very suitable. I can sleep for 7 hours in a row and sleep until dawn.
Secondly, the supporting facilities are perfect. There is unlimited supply of drinking water. Now that the weather is dry, how much water do I have to drink every day? Baiyun will put water directly at the service desk on each floor. If the service desk runs out of water at night, you can ask the waiter to deliver water the next day. This alone is much better than other hotels that only provide limited amount of drinking water.
The hair dryer is powerful and quiet. I want to buy one, but unfortunately the store said that this model is not on sale.
There is a locker rack at the entry, which is convenient for putting down the kettle in your hand when entering. The baby also used the luggage rack as a sleeping place.
It has been renovated for several years, so the hardware and furniture are not new. However, there are bedside reading lights, bedside emergency buttons, door opening alarms, etc. Traveling with a baby pays more attention to safety, and I feel that the hotel has spent the money on decoration to actually improve the comfort and safety of the stay.
There is a children's playground, suitable for young children to play.
I write so much because the staying experience this time is really good. If it is the same price, between the new chain hotel brand and the traditional hotel, next time I will choose the traditional hotel without hesitation.

There is a nucleic acid point within a ten-minute walking distance. The breakfast is on the 30th floor, self-service, the food is not too much but acceptable. It's just that the management of the restaurant needs to be strengthened, the tableware is placed as desired, and the tabletop is not clean.

Generally speaking, if you bring the elderly and children to Guangzhou in the future, you will still choose to book the supreme queen room of Baiyun Hotel.
